< text>
Have been trying to cool down in the 100°+F heat wave.  Decided to get a boba to cool off.  Stopped by at Cafe Tapioca.  As soon as you walk in, the place smells faintly of Sanrio's bubblegum erasers. Lol.. Brings back a lot of teenage memories.  Besides being a boba place, they also sell Snoopy cups, popular animation keychains, assorted Hi-Chew gums as well as snacks.  There are numerous games available to play when sit-in dining is allowed again.  Ordered a Pina Colada smoothie with tapioca pearls. Nice flavor and thickness despite it being pricier than other typical boba tea places.  Gotta try anyplace once. As a sidenote, there  is a sign that states this place gets sanitized by UV light.  Wonder how well UV light works to kill Covid 19?<//text>

< text>
The server was friendly and prepared our drinks promptly.  They even have Wifi, which is awesome!  And, there's not much of a line, and we easily found seats, among the less than dozen seats.  They picked a great location - the parking is easy and it's close to my house  =)

However, As a Milk tea aficionado, I was disappointed with the taste - it's not the best milk tea i've had - far from it.  My wife and I ordered the Regular tapioca milk tea and the Strawberry milk tea.  The milk tea was a bit tasteless, and the strawberry milk tea tasted nothing like any strawberry milk tea I've ever had, not in a good way.  Perhaps, they use less sugar in their recipe - this would be a good thing, if they at least had a nutritional label.  Without a label, you can't quantify it.  Quickly's tastes better, even when ordered with half sugar.  The tapioca balls were mushy and stuck together at the bottom of the drink.  With their unusually flattened straws, it made it hard to suck out even the normal tapioca balls.  The decoration isn't great either - the couch looks cold and unwelcoming.  And like many such places, they don't even offer a bathroom.  I think 3 stars is being generous.  Sorry... I wanted to like this place.

Keep working on the recipe - this place has potential.</text>

(Translated by Google) Salt Crisp Chicken Review Second Store, Cafe Tapioca, Dublin

Chicken: Chicken breast and chicken leg meat, the taste of pickled can break into the chicken.

Sweet potato powder: The skin is crispy and can also lock in the moisture and taste of chicken marinated.

Salt and pepper: Slightly salty, without the refreshing and peppery notes of salt and pepper.

Paprika: To be the hottest, spicy, not fragrant, no soul, can't make the salty chicken so spicy.

Can recommend.

(Original)
盐酥鸡评测第二家店，Cafe Tapioca, Dublin

鸡肉: 鸡胸肉和鸡腿肉都有，腌制的味道能够謦入鸡肉之中。

红薯粉: 表皮酥脆，里面也能够锁住鸡肉腌制的水分和味道。

椒盐: 略微咸了一些，没有椒盐的清爽和椒香。

辣椒粉: 要了最辣的，会辣，不香，没有灵魂，无法让盐酥鸡辣到欲罢不能。

可以推荐。</Text>

When I started the process of looking for a dentist, there weren't that many showing up who took my insurance and I wasn't all that interested in driving too far outside my geography. This year, more dentists were added, so I started the lengthy process of looking for a dentist who had the "least worst" review since there were no good reviews. And really, who wants to choose a dentist based on that, but I did.

When I set up my initial appointment, I had a three week wait to get in. Okay, not a big deal, I had gone years avoiding the dentist because of a really bad experience with a wallet gouger. When I arrived, after having read all the reviews, I was prepared for the worst.

Oh boy was I in for a surprise.

Granted, going to the dentist is not a fun experience for me and given how long I waited, I received a lengthy list of problems that needed to be resolved including a deep cleaning, two cavities, two crowns, and a night guard. As I'm reeling from the prognosis, I'm handed the estimated costs, which had me choking. The finance person offered to see if I qualified for Care Credit. I didn't think I would. She offered to try. Holy cow, I was approved! On top of that, they said they could start the process that day, when I was merely expecting to be evaluated and then brought back later (see comment above about last dentist). Now, in reading other reviews as well as some news piece about a lawsuit, understand that she went over everything with me, including the costs for each treatment, what was covered by my insurance, what would be out of pocket, everything. I knew what I was getting into when I signed up for the care card.

Now I have a chronic condition that does make pain tolerance difficult. I was impressed when the dentist told me that she worked with patients like me and they would go at my pace, not theirs. And given that I was fully numbed, I let them have free rein and we went for it. As in all of it. Full deep cleaning of the entire mouth (no pussy footing around quadrants at a time), two cavities filled and temporary crowns placed with an appointment for the permanent ones.

I was impressed with the team environment and how well everyone worked together. Okay, admittedly there are some negatives. The view in some of the stations isn’t quite as good as they could be. Given the amount of time I’ve spent in some of the chairs, it would be nice if they upgraded the chairs to include back massagers. Their taste in music is very similar to mine and I was at risk of hurting myself every time I found myself tapping my feet to the music while someone had his or her hands in my mouth with grinding, whirring, buzzing sounds. And the worst of them all, they’re human and prone to bad days too. And while I did get a bit of a “tone” when I called this morning as I was admonished for not cancelling/changing my appointment 24 hours in advance, I had an emergent situation come up this morning that prevented me from going and I was at a loss as to what to do. So, thank you for being so accommodating. Really.</text>

<time>1480343058966<//time>< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< review>
I lived in Hunan for more than five years. This food tastes the same. It's very authentic. But I only gave four stars because you have to serve yourself water from the water cooler across the room. It would be much better if they left a pitcher of water on the table. For faster service, you have to summon the waiters Chinese style (with a loud voice). Don't be shy. It's just a cultural difference. The prices are reasonable and the portions are large enough. There's plenty of parking outside, but be prepared to wait in line a bit during peak hours. If you like spicy, order the frog.</review>

Rod Gullo< /user_name>
< time>

< Rate>
1</Rate>
< Text>
Overpriced poor quality food, not at all like in China.  I have visited Beijing, Xi'an, Yichang, Shanghai, and Zhengzhou in China. The restaurants where the locals eat in each of these areas have excellent food prepared by owners who take pride in the quality and preparation of their food.  They serve some of the best food I have ever eaten with large portions, fresh ingredients, and fair prices.  Village Kitchen is the opposite.  The food is bland and every corner is cut to maximize profits.  The lamb pictured in the menu shows chunks, however what is served is miniscule shavings of lamb like the wood shavings from a pencil sharpener.  The only flavor of the lamb dish was an overabundance of cooking oil.  When I got home my body decided to reject the meal from both ends. My wife ordered the pork stomach which was also bland and priced double that of better quality restaurants.  If you are planning to spend at least $50 for two people, a way better meal can be had at the many better Chinese restaurants in San Diego like Chins and Chuns.</Text>

None<//pics>
< Text>
This is one of my favorite Chinese places in San Diego, alongside Village North.  They serve Hunan cuisine which is known for its spiciness and unforgiving assault of flavors on the palate, so be prepared for a heavy tasting meal and perhaps lots of rice and ice water!

Some of the highlights here include the preserved pork--I like it both in the stir fry and in the dry pot.  The stir fry can be a tad dry at times, but the fresh garlic leaves more than make up for that, and the dry pot is just so flavorful with the smoked bamboos, giving the dish as smoky of a flavor as you will ever find in Chinese food (which should appeal to any BBQ fans out there).  Chairman Mao's braised pork is quite good, similar to many other braised pork dishes, with a fermented bean curd flavor, as is common in the braised pork of certain Chinese (non Shanghainese) cuisines.  The deboned pork rib with fried egg casserole is actually one of the milder dishes on the menu in terms of flavor, but not in terms of spiciness! It's one that I enjoy very much as well for some lighter dishes to balance the others.  On the other hand, the pickled chilli with pork is quite a spicy dish, with the aromas of the chilli pepper making the dish very very good.

Of the non-pork dishes, the Chef's Beef Brisket is quite good, a little bit reminiscent of beef noodle soups except served as a dish without noodles and soup.  The mapo tofu is a simple but very flavorful dish with plenty of Sichuan peppercorns to numb your tongue.  The steamed egg here is possibly one of my favorite steamed eggs I've had, with some good flavors and a very good texture on the egg--not over or underdone.  The eggplant with green chilli and century egg dish is one of their signatures for a reason.  The flavors are very balanced with the eggplant serving as a good base.

I could probably go on about the other dishes since there really hasn't been many that have disappointed me.  I highly recommend coming with a group of people to order and try more dishes and seeing which you enjoy the most!  I also noticed that the dishes tend to be spicier in the summer, since perhaps it fluctuates with the spiciness of the chilli peppers which may be seasonal, so if you want to give yourself a challenge, definitely come during that time.</Text>

Sidney Kuo</username>

< text>
Real Chinese food. The food has the potential to be better, but this style of cooking is not easy to come by in San Diego and is good enough for me to come back regularly. Particular favourites: kourou (pork belly), mashed pidan and eggplant, taro and radish soup, among others. Note: the tudousi (potato matchsticks in vinegar) are pretty spicy here.</text>

<text>This place was recommended by one of our foodie friends so I had decent expectations coming in. I found out later that there was one particular dish he was a fan of - the mashed eggplant with century egg. Comes with a giant mortar and pestle that looked pretty neat and was the best mix of flavors in an eggplant dish I've ever had if not the biggest portion. Most of the other dishes were just average (braised pork), lacking in flavor (fried rice), or just came with a higher price when compared with other places such as Chef Chin or Szechuan Chef.

Since I'm a fan of tea we also tried the Dragon Well and Oosmanthus Oolong teas which looked like they were loose leaf but somehow still lacked flavor, perhaps they had been recycled?

Food did come out quickly though and service was pretty good for a Chinese place - we were in and out in about an hour. If you're really into Hunan cuisine, you might like it more but otherwise I would consider it a maybe try once kind of place.< /text>< Pics>

I have had the opportunity and travel to various Fit Republics throughout the Central Valley, Central Coast, and North Valley areas through Sacramento.

I find the Riverbank Fit Republic more appealing than most.  It is quaint and smaller than most facilities, however has everything I need for weight training and cardio workouts.  I have met a 95-year old gentlemen, 86- year wonderful lady, Baby Boomers, Generation X, Generation Z, Traditionalists, and Millennial's here.  ¬¬¬¬¬¬¬

The manager and staff are very friendly.  There has been a change from a corporate unit to a franchise unit. I have noticed the following changes.

* Upgraded Equipment
* Overall cleanliness
* Timely service on equipment needing attention
* Improvement on regular maintenance

I have met the new owners.  They are professional, courteous and customer oriented.

This is a friendly and safe environment.  If you are looking for a good workout.....Bring It!

A five star rating would be for several lockers needing repair.  A few details and minor aesthetics needing attention.  It is my personal favorite of all the Fit Republics I have traveled too from the Central Coast through the Valley (Los Banos, Merced) and North to Manteca & Stockton.< /text>

< username>
JR Curley< /username>
<date>1465765723950</date><rate>3<//rate>< review>
This is a super small Starbucks located on the USC campus. The spot itself hosts all of the traditional coffee and food other Starbuck locations offer, but the actual square footage is quite small. There are no seats inside, only outside, and none of them come with power ports. The staff are friendly and fast, but waves of students can come and they can get overwhelmed. The outside seating location comprises of several non-moveable metal tables and chairs.

Pro tip - don't sit outside the Starbucks, instead look at the space in front of the Leavey Library or on the quad.<//review>

Like this store alot.

< review>
I've never left a review before but this company is certainly deserving of one. Very professional, very quick, and even more friendly. My initial test failed because the check engine light had just been reset. Rather than just turn me away, take my money and tell me to come back later, the tester fully explained why the test failed. He then explained how to fix the issue. I had to drive around until all the computers reset themselves after you reset the check engine light. Fortunately, I own the computer you plug in to tell you when all is good. If you don't have one, the shop will rent one out. I drove around for awhile at at 4:50 everything was good. I called back and even though they close at 5, the tester said he would stay open and wait for me to get back. I arrived after closing time and he was still there, completed the testing and provided me with the report. Not only is this a very professional establishment, it was also the lowest cost as he provided me with a coupon. I ended up paying 45 dollars for everything. Other places I asked charged 60 or over. Please use this business for your smog check. They deserve it. The only complaint I have is that a smog test is only done once a year and I won't be able to experience such great service until the next one is due.< /review>
